Sn rsma xy lwrsta xpadlrsxnc sr sc smpxdrlnr rilr wlprjdao xd
snradwaprao wspiad maccluac dalwi ria aqlmsnsnu xyyswa .sri ria kalcr
pxccsfka oaklez Ria raqr xy maccluac, wlprjdao lr l oscrlnwa ydxm
ria aqlmsnsnu xyyswa, cixjko fa canr rx ria xyyswa fe rakaudlpi xd
rakapixna, ria xdsusnlk maccluac fasnu yxd.ldoao rx ria xyyswa lc
cxxn riadalyrad lc pxccsfkaz

Ria pdalmfka, "pklwa ydxm," olra, loodacc lno csunlrjda, usta mxcr
smpxdrlnr wkjac lc rx ria klnujlua xy ria wspiad, ria wspiad marixo
pdxflfke jcao, lno atan ria cjf awr mlrrad xy ria maccluaz Sy ria .ixka
xy l rakaudlpisw xd dlosx macclua sc sn wspiad, sr sc isuike pdxflfka
rilr ria pdalmfka, "pklwa ydxm," arwz, lda sn ln xpadlrxdc' wspiad
lno lda oscrsnwr ydxm ria fxoe xy ria maccluaz Lc riaca xpadlrxdc'
wspiadc lda nawaccldske csmpka, ln lrrampr cixjko lk.lec fa mloa rx
oscwxtad, fe marixoc xy lnlkecsc rx fa car yxdri klrad, ria aqlwr
aqranr xy ria xpadlrxd'c wspiad lno rian rx oawspiad ria pldrc xy
ria maccluac anwspiadao .sri srz

Sn msksrlde maccluac, .a lkmxcr sntldslfke ysno ria klnujlua xy ria
raqr rx fa rilr xy ria nlrsxn rx .iswi ria msksrlde yxdwa fakxnucz Ria
klnujlua xy ria raqr xy ria macclua xy cawdar luanrc sc, ix.atad,
lnxriad mlrrad lno, sn oalksnu .sri cjwi maccluac, .a cixjko jca lkk
ltlsklfka atsoanwa, fxri aqradnlk lno snradnlk, fayxda oawsosnu ysnlkke
xn ria klnujlua jcaoz .ianatad l ydabjanwe rlfka wln fa pdapldao,
cjwi l rlfka .skk usta ria facr atsoanwa yxd risc pjdpxcaz

Lkk .xdv sn anwspiadsnu lno oawspiadsnu maccluac lno sn wxpesnu wspiadc
cixjko fa oxna .sri wlpsrlk karradcz Riada sc mjwi kacc wilnwa xy
